GRW_republican_politics = {
	#建立埃维联合社会主义共和国
	GRW_form_Evi = {
		icon = griffon
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GRW_form_Evi_flag
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRW_united_front
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = GRW_form_Evi_tt

						exists = no
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT

						exists = no

						is_in_faction_with = ROOT

							state = 446
						}

				}
			}
			else = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = GRW_Evi_cores

					limit = {

					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
			GRY = {
				if = {

						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = {
						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes
				GRY_cornilo_khurshevich = {
					set_nationality = ROOT

						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {

		icon = griffon

		allowed = {

		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 671
				CYA = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GRW_establish_minotaur_autonomous_region_flag
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_establish_minotaur_autonomous_region_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = CYA_cores
					owner = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
			}
			CYA = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = {
						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes
				CYA_ersuhl_von_thymiaushafen = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = CYA_cores
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = GRW_minotaur_autonomous_government
						}
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = GRW_minotaur_autonomous_government
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = CYA_cores
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = GRW_minotaur_autonomous_region
				}
			}
		}
	}

					set_nationality = ROOT
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_unit_leader = no
						}
						add_corps_commander_role = {
							desc = edgy_commie_bird_desc
							traits = {
								griffon_race_trait
								inspirational_leader
								promising_general
								irregulars_officer
							}
							skill = 2

							defense_skill = 2
							planning_skill = 3
							logistics_skill = 1
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_advisor_role = {
							slot = army_chief
						}
						add_advisor_role = {
							advisor = {
								slot = army_chief
								cost = 100

								ledger = army

								cost = 100

								traits = {
									army_infantry_2
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			GFF = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = {
						annex_country = {
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = GRF_cores
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}

	#将领地移交给黑空平等主义实验区
	GRW_give_state_to_BAN_equalism_autonomous_region = {
		icon = infiltrate_state
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		visible = {
			any_state = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = GRW_BAN_equalism_autonomous_region
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = GRW_BAN_equalism_autonomous_region
					}
				}
			}
		}

		state_target = any_owned_state
		target_array = owned_controlled_states
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_state_flag = BAN_cores
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = GRW_BAN_equalism_autonomous_region
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#工业原材料增长
	GRW_mission_construction_materials_growth = {
		icon = clock_decision
		priority = 999

		allowed = {
			always = no
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 30

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_construction_materials_growth_tt
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GRW_var_construction_materials
				value = GRW_var_construction_materials_growth
			}
			activate_mission = GRW_mission_construction_materials_growth
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = GRW_national_construction_directorate_1
						has_idea = GRW_national_construction_directorate_2
						has_idea = GRW_national_construction_directorate_3
						has_idea = GRW_national_construction_directorate_4
					}
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = GRW_invest_stateowned_company
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					15 = {
						GRW_syndicalism_influence_slightincrease = yes
					}
					85 = {
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#进口工业原材料
	GRW_import_materials = {
		icon = generic_wreckers
		cost = 40
		days_remove = 60

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}

		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.1
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_import_materials_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = GRW_var_construction_materials
					value = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#出口工业原材料
	GRW_export_materials = {
		icon = generic_nationalism
		cost = 0

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = GRW_export_materials_tt
				check_variable = {
					GRW_var_construction_materials > 49
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {#关闭
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GRW_export_materials_flag
				}
				clr_country_flag = GRW_export_materials_flag
				custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_export_materials_disable_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_mission = GRW_mission_export_materials
					remove_ideas = GRW_export_materials_idea
				}
			}
			else = {#开启
				set_country_flag = GRW_export_materials_flag
				custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_export_materials_enable_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = GRW_mission_export_materials
					add_ideas = GRW_export_materials_idea
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#出口工业原材料任务
	GRW_mission_export_materials = {
		icon = generic_nationalism

		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			always = no
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				check_variable = {
					GRW_var_construction_materials < 50
				}
			}
		}

		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 45

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_50_Materials
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GRW_var_construction_materials
				value = 50
			}
			add_political_power = 45
			activate_mission = GRW_mission_export_materials
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = GRW_export_materials_flag
				remove_mission = GRW_mission_export_materials
				remove_ideas = GRW_export_materials_idea
			}
		}
	}

			508 = {

			}
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
		}

			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = GRW_var_reconstruction_cost_negative
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = GRW_var_construction_materials
					value = 50
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			508 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 16
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_var_construction_materials_growth5_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = GRW_var_construction_materials_growth
					value = 5

	GRW_promote_land_reform_auto = {#自动进行土改
		icon = generic_agriculture
		cost = 0

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRW_promote_prywhen_model
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_flag
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				land_reform_allow_up = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_flag
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = GRW_mission_promote_land_reform_auto
				add_ideas = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_cost
			}
		}
	}
	GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_cancel = {#取消自动进行土改
		icon = generic_agriculture
		cost = 0

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRW_promote_prywhen_model
			has_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_flag
		}

		complete_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_flag
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_mission = GRW_mission_promote_land_reform_auto
				remove_ideas = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_cost
			}
		}
	}
	GRW_mission_promote_land_reform_auto = {#自动土改任务
		icon = generic_agriculture

		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			always = no
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			land_reform_allow_up = no
		}

		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 90

		timeout_effect = {
			add_political_power = -15
			add_stability = 0.01
			activate_mission = GRW_mission_promote_land_reform_auto
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_flag
						has_state_flag = GRW_cores
						has_state_category = large_town
						has_state_category = city
						has_state_category = large_city
						has_state_category = metropolis
						has_state_category = megalopolis
					}
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_flag
				improve_state_category = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					add_compliance = 3
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_cost
				}
				remove_ideas = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_cost
			}
			clr_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_flag
		}
	}
	GRW_promote_land_reform_hidden = {#隐藏土改决议
		icon = generic_decision
		days_remove = SNL_var_days_test?1

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRW_promote_prywhen_model
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_hidden_flag
				has_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_flag

	#在各个自治共和国进行土地改革
	GRW_promote_land_reform = {
		icon = generic_agriculture
		cost = 5
		days_remove = 90
		on_map_mode = map_only

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRW_promote_prywhen_model
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_hidden_flag
				has_country_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_auto_flag
			}
			FROM = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_flag
					has_state_flag = GRW_cores
					has_state_category = large_town
					has_state_category = city
					has_state_category = large_city
					has_state_category = metropolis
					has_state_category = megalopolis
				}
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		state_target = any_owned_state
		target_array = owned_controlled_states
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_state_flag = GRW_Evi_cores
					has_state_flag = CYA_cores
					has_state_flag = WNG_cores
					has_state_flag = FAL_cores
					has_state_flag = SIC_cores
					has_state_flag = TAL_cores
					has_state_flag = FRN_cores
					has_state_flag = ARA_cores
					has_state_flag = HLQ_cores
					has_state_flag = GRW_Central_Griffonia_cores
					has_state_flag = BOI_cores
					has_state_flag = GRW_Western_Griffonia_cores
					has_state_flag = FAT_cores
					has_state_flag = MNC_cores
					has_state_flag = VED_cores
					has_state_flag = SRS_cores
					has_state_flag = HAU_cores
					has_state_flag = GRF_cores
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.05
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.05
		}
		remove_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.01
			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = GRW_promote_land_reform_flag
				improve_state_category = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					add_compliance = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

				remove_idea = GRW_free_medical_care_idea_2
				add_idea = GRW_free_medical_care_idea_3
			}
			decrease_poverty = yes
		}
	}
}

#通用政治行动
political_actions = {
	#显示历史类决议
	GRW_decision_show_history_decisions = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = GRW_history_of_Prywhen_hidden_flag
		}

		complete_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GRW_history_of_Prywhen_hidden_flag
		}
	}
	#隐藏历史类决议
	GRW_decision_hide_history_decisions = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GRW
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GRW_history_of_Prywhen_hidden_flag
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GRW_history_of_Prywhen_hidden_flag
		}
	}

	#压制共产主义影响
	RIV_remove_agitators_decision = {
		icon = anti_communist
		cost = 75
		days_remove = 120

		allowed = {
			is_original_riv_fed_country_tag = yes
		}
		visible = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = RCT_has_agitators
				OR = {
					has_idea = GRW_communist_infiltrators
					has_idea = GRW_communist_infiltrators_NIM
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			political_power_cost = 0.2
		}
		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = RIV_remove_agitators_decision_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GRW_communist_infiltrators
				}
				remove_ideas = GRW_communist_infiltrators
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GRW_communist_infiltrators_NIM
				}
				remove_ideas = GRW_communist_infiltrators_NIM
			}
		}
	}
}
